PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government Notifications
SRI   LANKA   INSTITUTE   OF   ARCHITECTS
NEW Registration and Renewal of Registration of “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates”
for the year 2016/2017 under the Architects Registration Board, established as per the Sri Lanka Institute of Arachitects
(Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996.
REFERENCE is made to the notes appearing on pages 1A, 2A, 3A, 4A and 5A of the Gazette of the Democratic
Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka  ( Extraordinary ) No. 1015/19 of Friday, the 20th February, 1998 with regard to the
Registration of persons who are eligible to practice Architecture in Sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered Archi-
tects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates”. The interpretations of the Sri Lanka Institute of Archietects (Amend-
ment) Act, No. 14 of 1996 in the above Gazette Notification will apply in all respects to the list published below.
The Architects Registration Board of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects as per the functions and powers vested
upon it by the said Act. of Parliament, has now prepared the list of the “Chartered Architects”, ”Architects” and “Architec-
tural Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazetted for the year 2016/2017 (01st February, 2016 to 31st January, 2017).
The Architects Registration Board directed me to publish the Names, Addresses and Registration Numbers of the
“Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” who have been registered as given below.
This registration expires on 31st January, 2017.
E. G. G . M. E
LLEPOLAGEDARA,
Registrar,
Architects Registration Board.
Sri Lanka Institute of Architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha,
Colombo 07,
18th January 2016.
